;(
; ----------------------- Attributes ----------------------- 

(
(cat		; main POS category:
	  Verb	; verb
	  NomC	; common noun
	  NomP	; proper noun
	  AdjQ	; adjective
	  Pron	; pronoun
	  Dete	; determiner
	  Ordi	; ordinal
	  Quan	; quantifier
	  Prep	; preposition
	  Punc	; punctuation
	  Adve	; adverb
	  ConC	; coordinate conjunction
	  ConS	; subordinate conjuntion
	  Inte	; interjection
	  Affi	; affix
	  Post	; post-head particule
	  PreH	; pre-head particle (not yet implemented.  For "miss", etc)
	  Disc	; Discourse markers (NB, PS, etc)
	  Ltre	; alphabet
)
(PostType	; post-head particle type
	  time	; follows a construction time headed (eg GMT)
	  degr  ; follows a type "unit" construction (eg 34 degree Fahrenheit)
	  orgn	; follows a type "organisim" construction (eg Pepe et fils inc.)
)
(VerbType	; verb type
	  lex	; lexical verb
	  auxt	; auxiliary verb
	  moda	; modal verb
)
(NomPType	; proper noun type
	  pgeo	;geographical (Canada)
	  phum	; personal names (John, Crosbie)
	  porg	; organizations (Globe and Mail)
)
(DeteType	; determiner type
	  dart	; article (a, an, the)
	  dpos	; possessive deter (her, his, its, my, our, their, thy, your)
	  ddem	; demonstrative determiner (that, these, this, those)
	  dwdt	; WH-word (what, whate'er, whatever)
)
(PronType	; pronoun type
	  prp	; personal pronoun (he, her, hers)
	  prfl	; reflexive pronoun (herself, himself)
	  pdm	; demonstrative pronoun (that, these this, those)
	  pid	; indefinite pronoun (another, anybody)
	  pwhr	; relative pronoun (that, when)
	  pwhi	; interrogative pronoun (how, what)
	  pex	; existential pronoun (there)
)
(QuanCla	; quantifier class
	  num	; numerals (two, four)
	  frc	; fractions (one-half)
	  cmp	; comparative (more, less)	???
	  sup	; superlative (most, least)	??? VS Forme(Compar, Super).
	  ndg	; number degree (all, some)
	  pos	; positive degree (few, many)
)
(PrepType	; preposition type
	  TO	; "to" infinitive
	  RP	; adverbial particule
)
(AdveType	; adverb type
	  XNOT	; negation (not)
	  nomi	; (downstairs)
	  part	; particule (back)
)
(ConCType	; preposition type
	  Dble	; (both..and, either..or)
)
(AbbrCla	; abbreviation Class
	  MD	; discourse particle (NB, eg)
	  PT	; problematic word (Celsius, BC)
)
(Typo		; typography
	  cap	; begin by a capital letter
)
(PuncType	; punctuation mark:
	  pcst	; full-stop (.)
	  pccm	; comma (,)
	  pcsc	; semicolon (;)
	  pcco	; colon (:)
	  pcql	; left quote (``)
	  pcqr	; right quote ('')
	  pcpl	; left paren [(]
	  pcpr	; right paren [)]
	  pcda	; dash (-)
	  pcdd	; dots (...)
	  pcsl	; slash (/)
)
(tem		; verb tense
	  BSE	; base form
	  PAST	; past form
	  PRES	; present form
	  PRP	; present participle
	  PSP	; past participle
)
(Gen		; grammatical gender
	  femi	; feminine
	  gmfn	; masculine, feminine or masculine
	  mafe	; masculine or feminine
	  masc	; masculine
	  neut	; neuter
)
(Nbr		; grammatical number
	  sing	; singular (he)
	  plur	; plural (they)
	  sgpl	; singular or plural
)
(Per		; person
	  p1	; 1st (we, my)
	  p2	; 2nd (you, your)
	  p3	; 3rd (they, its)
)
(QuanPos	; quantifier position
	  SAhn	; QT After Head-Noun ( NomC QT )
	  SPdt	; QT Pre-DeTerminer (QT Dete NomC)
	  SPhn	; QT-comparatif Pre-modifiant un Head-Noun
	  SPjr	; QT Pre-modifiant un [AdjQ | Adve | Quan] comparatif
	  SPqt	; QT-comparatif Pre-modifiant un [AdjQ | Adve]
	  Sprn	; QT PRoNoun position
	  Sdet	; QT DETerminer ( QT au-lieu-de Dete_dart_def )
	  Sh_n	; QT Head-Noun position
	  Sord	; QT ORDdinal (QT au-lieu-de Ordi)
)
(Cas		; case
	  cno	; nominative or objective
	  gen	; genitive
	  ngo	; nominative, objective or genitive
	  nom	; nominative
	  obj	; objective
)
(posi		; adjective distribution
	  posU	; position unknown
	  attr	; attributive
	  pred	; predicative
	  atpr	; attributive or predicative
)
(forme		; 
	  Compar	; forme comparative
	  Super	; forme superlative
)
(Typ		; type
	  def	; definite
	  ind	; indefinite
)
(Str		; string
	  car	; caracter (four, fifth)
)
(Join		; join by
	  hyphen	; an hyphen
)
(cnt		; count
	  yes	; yes
	  no	; no
	  both	; both yes and no
)
(Own		; owner
	  osp	; singular or plural
	  plu	; plural
	  sng	; singular
)
(arg		; syntactical argument
	  ArgX	; unapplicable
	  intr	; intransitive
	  trans	; transitive
	  trin	; transitive and intransitive
)
(Ref		; refer to
	  bh	; somebody or something
	  rb	; adverbial (time, maner, cause)
	  sb	; somebody
	  sh	; something
)
(Nbc		; combines with a noun which is
	  c+u	; count or uncount
	  cnt	; count
	  unc	; uncount
)
(Elider		; word which causes a->an (hour)
	med
)
)

; ----------------------- Inflection Rules -----------------------

; Determiners rules:


(d1 "a"
	("a" dart ind unc sing)
	("an" dart ind unc sing)
	("the" dart def c+u sgpl)
)
(d2 "my"
	(my dpos def c+u p1 sgpl mafe sng)
	(thy dpos def p2 sing)
	(your dpos def c+u p2 sgpl mafe osp)
	(her dpos def c+u p3 sgpl femi sng)
	(his dpos def c+u p3 sgpl masc sng)
	(its dpos def c+u p3 sgpl neut sng)
	(our dpos def c+u p1 sgpl mafe plu)
	(their dpos def c+u p3 sgpl mafe plu)
)
(d3 "that"
	(that ddem ind c+u sing)
	(this ddem def c+u sing)
	(those ddem ind cnt plur)
	(these ddem def cnt plur)
)
(d4 ""	("" dwdt c+u sgpl))

; Pronouns rules:

(pn1 "I"
	(I p1 sing mafe)
	(you p2 sgpl mafe)
	(he p3 sing masc)
	(it p3 sing neut)
	(she p3 sing femi)
	(one p3 sing neut)
	(we p1 plur mafe)
	(they p3 plur gmfn)
)
(pn2 "me"
	(me p1 sing mafe)
	(you p2 sgpl mafe)
	(her p3 sing femi)
	(him p3 sing masc)
	(it p3 sing neut)
	(us p1 plur mafe)
	(them p3 plur gmfn)
)
(pn3 "mine"
	(mine p1 sgpl mafe sng)
	(yours p2 sgpl mafe osp)
	(hers p3 sgpl femi sng)
	(his p3 sgpl masc sng)
	(its p3 sgpl neut sng)
	(ours p1 sgpl mafe plu)
	(theirs p3 sgpl gmfn plu)
)
(pn4 "myself"
	(myself p1 sing mafe)
	(ourself p1 sing mafe) ; myself
	(yourself p2 sing mafe)
	(herself p3 sing femi)
	(himself p3 sing masc)
	(itself p3 sing neut)
	(oneself p3 sing neut)
	(ourselves p1 plur mafe)
	(yourselves p2 plur mafe)
	(themselves p3 plur gmfn)
)
(pn5 ""	("" pid cno p3))
(pn6 ""	("" pwhi))
(pn7 ""	("" pwhr))
(pn8 ""	("" pdm))
(pn9 ""	("" pex))

(pp ""	(""))

; Punctuation

("."    pc Punc pcst)
(":"    pc Punc pcco)
(")"    pc Punc pcpr)
("("    pc Punc pcpl)
("?"    pc Punc pcst)
("--"   pc Punc pcda)
("..."  pc Punc pcdd)
("!"    pc Punc pcst)
(";"    pc Punc pcsc)
("'"    pc Punc pcqr)
("'"    pc Punc pcql)

("["    pc Punc pcpl)
('"'    pc Punc pcqr)
('"'    pc Punc pcql)

("''"   pc Punc pcqr)
("``"   pc Punc pcql)
("/"	pc Punc pcsl)
